Please run SQL script.\");\n                  return;\n              }\n          }\n          if (data) setOrders(data.map(d => ({\n              ...d, \n              customerName: d.customer_name, \n              customerPhone: d.customer_phone, \n              totalAmount: d.total_amount,\n              netAmount: d.net_amount || d.total_amount,\n              createdAt: d.created_at,\n              deliveryAddress: d.delivery_address,\n              deliveryZone: d.delivery_zone,\n              deliveryFee: d.delivery_fee,\n              paymentMethod: d.payment_method,\n              pickupTime: d.pickup_time,\n              tableNumber: d.table_number\n          })));\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Orders fetch failed\", err); // Reload orders when change happens\n        })\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'menu_items' }, fetchMenu)\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'store_settings' }, fetchSettings)\n        .subscribe();\n        \n        // Polling fallback every 5 seconds to ensure status updates even if realtime is flaky\n        const interval = setInterval(() => {\n             fetchOrders();\n        }, 5000);\n        \n        return () => { \n            subscription.unsubscribe(); \n            clearInterval(interval);\n        }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update customer profile on load if logged in\n  useEffect(() => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured && customer) {\n          fetchCustomerProfile();\n      }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Actions\n  const addPizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').insert([{\n                id: pizza.id, name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }]);\n          } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\n      } \n      // Always update local state for immediate feedback\n      setMenu(prev => [...prev, pizza]);\n  };\n  const updatePizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').update({\n                name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }).eq('id', pizza.id);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      // Always update local\n      setMenu(prev => prev.map(p => p.id === pizza.id ? pizza : p));\n  };\n  const deletePizza = async (id: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try { await supabase.from('menu_items').delete().eq('id', id); } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setMenu(prev => prev.filter(p => p.id !== id));\n  };\n  const updatePizzaPrice = async (id: string, newPrice: number) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) await updatePizza({ ...p, basePrice: newPrice });\n  };\n  const togglePizzaAvailability = async (id: string) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) await updatePizza({ ...p, available: !p.available });\n  };\n  const toggleBestSeller = async (id: string) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) {\n          const newVal = !p.isBestSeller;\n          if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n              try {\n                await supabase.from('menu_items').update({ is_best_seller: newVal }).eq('id', id);\n              } catch(e) { console.error(e); Cannot upload.\");\n          return;\n      }\n      const confirmUpload = window.confirm(\"This will upload all the latest Menu Items and Toppings from the code to the Database. It will overwrite existing items with the same ID. Continue?\");\n      if (!confirmUpload) return;\n\n      try {\n          // Upload Menu\n          for (const p of INITIAL_MENU) {\n              const { error } = await supabase.from('menu_items').upsert({\n                  id: p.id, name: p.name, name_th: p.nameTh, \n                  base_price: p.basePrice, description: p.description, \n                  description_th: p.descriptionTh, image: p.image, \n                  category: p.category, available: p.available, \n                  is_best_seller: p.isBestSeller, combo_count: p.comboCount\n              });\n              if (error) {\n                  if (error.code === '42703') {\n                      alert(\"Database Error: Column missing. Please run the SQL script provided in the Supabase SQL Editor to update your table structure.\");\n                      return;\n                  }\n                  console.error(\"Menu Seed Error\", error);\n              }\n          }\n          // Upload Toppings\n          for (const t of INITIAL_TOPPINGS) {\n              // Try catch for category column specifically (in case user schema is old)\n              try {\n                  const { error } = await supabase.from('toppings').upsert({\n                      id: t.id, name: t.name, name_th: t.nameTh, price: t.price,\n                      category: t.category \n                  });\n                  if (error) throw error;\n              } catch (e: any) {\n                  if (e.code === '42703') {\n                      alert(\"Database Error: Column missing. Please run the SQL script.\");\n                      return;\n                  }\n                  // Fallback: Try without category if column missing\n                   await supabase.from('toppings').upsert({\n                      id: t.id, name: t.name, name_th: t.nameTh, price: t.price\n                  });\n              }\n          }\n          alert(\"Menu uploaded to database successfully! Your app is now in sync.\");\n          fetchMenu(); // Refresh\n          fetchToppings(); // Refresh\n      } catch (err) {\n          console.error(\"Seeding failed\", err);\n          alert(\"Seeding failed. Check console for details.\");\n      }\n  };\n\n  const addTopping = async (topping: Topping) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await CartItem) => setCart(prev => [...prev, item]);\n  const updateCartItemQuantity = (itemId: string, delta: number) => {\n      setCart(prev => prev.map(item => {\n          if (item.id === itemId) {\n              const newQty = Math.max(1, item.quantity + delta);\n              return { ...item, quantity: newQty, totalPrice: (item.totalPrice / item.quantity) * newQty };\n          }\n          return item;\n      }));\n  };\n  const updateCartItem = (updatedItem: CartItem) => {\n      setCart(prev => prev.map(item => item.id === updatedItem.id ? updatedItem : item));\n  };\n  const removeFromCart = (itemId: string) => setCart(prev => prev.filter(item => item.id !== itemId));\n  const clearCart = () => setCart([]);\n  const cartTotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.totalPrice, 0);\n\n  // Customer\n  const setCustomer = async (profile: CustomerProfile) => {\n      setCustState(profile);\n      localStorage.setItem('damac_customer', JSON.stringify(profile));\n      // Sync to DB\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            const payload: any = {\n                phone: profile.phone, \n                name: profile.name, \n                address: profile.address, \n                birthday: profile.birthday,\n                password: profile.password, // Save password\n                loyalty_points: profile.loyaltyPoints, \n                tier: profile.tier,\n                saved_favorites: profile.savedFavorites, \n                order_history: profile.orderHistory\n            };\n            \n            if (profile.pdpaAccepted !== undefined) payload.pdpa_accepted = profile.pdpaAccepted;\n            if (profile.savedAddresses !== undefined) payload.saved_addresses = profile.savedAddresses;\n\n            await supabase.from('customers').upsert(payload);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Customer sync failed\", e); }\n      }\n  };\n  \n  // Smart Register / Reset Password\n  const registerCustomer = async (newProfile: CustomerProfile): Promise<'created' | 'updated'> => {\n      let existingPoints = 0;\n      let existingHistory: string[] = [];\n      let existingFavorites: SavedFavorite[] = [];\n      let existingTier: 'Bronze' | 'Silver' | 'Gold' | undefined = undefined;\n      let action: 'created' | 'updated' = 'created';\n\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          // Check if user exists\n          try {\n              const { data } = await supabase.from('customers').select('*').eq('phone', newProfile.phone).single();\n              if (data) {\n                  // User exists! Preserve their valuable data\n                  action = 'updated';\n                  existingPoints = data.loyalty_points || 0;\n                  existingHistory = data.order_history || [];\n                  existingFavorites = data.saved_favorites || [];\n                  existingTier = data.tier;\n              }\n          } catch (e) { console.warn(\"Error checking existing customer\", e); }\n      }\n\n      // Merge new details with existing history\n      const finalProfile: CustomerProfile = {\n          ...newProfile,\n          loyaltyPoints: existingPoints,\n          orderHistory: existingHistory,\n          savedFavorites: existingFavorites,\n          tier: existingTier\n      };\n      \n      await setCustomer(finalProfile);\n      return action;\n  };\n  \n  const getAllCustomers = async () => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) return [];\n      try {\n          const { data, error } = await supabase.from('customers').select('name, phone, loyalty_points, Birthday: c.birthday,\n              Address: c.address ? c.address.replace(/[\\n,]/g, ' ') : '', // Escape commas\n              OrdersCount: c.order_history ? c.order_history.length : 0\n          }));\n      } catch (e) {\n          console.error(\"Export failed\", e);\n          return [];\n      }\n  };\n  \n  const customerLogin = async (phone: string, password: string): Promise<boolean> => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          // If DB is offline, check local storage or basic bypass for demo purposes\n          const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_customer');\n          if (saved) {\n              const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);\n              if (parsed.phone === phone) { // Very basic \"offline\" check\n                  setCustState(parsed);\n                  return true;\n              }\n          }\n          alert(\"Database not connected and no local profile found.\");\n          return false;\n      }\n      try {\n          const { data, error } = {\n          console.error(\"Login failed\", e);\n      }\n      return false;\n  };\n\n  const addToFavorites = async (name: string, pizzaId: string, toppings: Topping[]) => {\n      if (!customer) if (order) {\n          order.items.forEach(item => {\n              addToCart({ ...item, id: Date.now().toString() + Math.random() }); // New ID for new cart item\n          });\n      }\n  };\n addToCart({\n          id: 'reward-' + Date.now(),\n          pizzaId: pizza.id,\n          name: `🏆 FREE ${pizza.name}`,\n          nameTh: `🏆 ฟรี ${pizza.nameTh || pizza.name}`,\n          basePrice: 0,\n          selectedToppings: [],\n          quantity: 1,\n          totalPrice: 0\n      });\n      // Deduct points\n      const updated = { ...customer, loyaltyPoints: customer.loyaltyPoints - 10 };\n      setCustomer(updated);\n      return true;\n  };\n\n  // Orders\n  const placeOrder = async (type: OrderType, details: any = {}): Promise<boolean> => {\n    // If DB is offline, we proceed with local state to allow the app to function as a demo/offline POS\n    try {\n        const { note, delivery, paymentMethod, pickupTime, tableNumber, source = 'store' } = details;\n        \n        // Save address if new (only for store orders with a logged in customer)\n        if (source === 'store' && customer && type === 'delivery' && delivery?.address) {\n            const currentSaved = customer.savedAddresses || [];\n            if (!currentSaved.includes(delivery.address)) {\n                const newSavedAddresses = [...currentSaved, delivery.address];\n                // Note: setCustomer handles its own errors silently\n                try {\n                     await setCustomer({ ...customer, savedAddresses: newSavedAddresses, address: delivery.address });\n                } catch (e) { console.warn(\"Could not save address, continuing\", e); }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Calculate Net Revenue (Deduct GP)\n        const gpRate = GP_RATES[source as OrderSource] || 0;\n        const netAmount = cartTotal * (1 - gpRate);\n\n        const newOrder: Order = {\n            id: Date.now().toString(),\n            customerName: customer?.name || 'Guest',\n            customerPhone: customer?.phone || 'Guest',\n            type,\n            source: source,\n            status: source === 'store' ? 'pending' : 'confirmed', // 3rd party auto-confirmed\n            items: cart,\n            totalAmount: cartTotal,\n            netAmount: Math.round(netAmount || 0),\n            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n            note: note || '',\n            deliveryAddress: delivery?.address,\n            deliveryZone: delivery?.zoneName,\n            deliveryFee: delivery?.fee,\n            paymentMethod,\n            pickupTime,\n            tableNumber\n        };\n        \n        // SAVE ORDER ID TO LOCAL STORAGE FOR GUEST TRACKING\n        localStorage.setItem('damac_last_order', newOrder.id);\n\n        // Always update local state first for responsiveness\n        setOrders(prev => [newOrder, ...prev]);\n        \n        // Loyalty Points (Only for Store Orders)\n        if (customer && source === 'store') {\n            const pizzasCount = cart.filter(i => menu.find(m => m.id === i.pizzaId)?.category === 'pizza').length;\n            if (pizzasCount > 0) {\n                const updated = { \n                    ...customer, \n                    loyaltyPoints: customer.loyaltyPoints + pizzasCount,\n                    orderHistory: [newOrder.id, ...(customer.orderHistory || [])]\n                };\n                // setCustomer handles its own errors\n                try {\n                     await setCustomer(updated);\n                } catch(e) { console.warn(\"Could not update points\", e); }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Attempt DB Sync\n        if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n            try {\n                const { error } = await supabase.from('orders').insert([{\n                    id: newOrder.id,\n                    customer_name: newOrder.customerName,\n                    customer_phone: newOrder.customerPhone,\n                    type: newOrder.type,\n                    source: newOrder.source,\n                    status: newOrder.status,\n                    total_amount: newOrder.totalAmount,\n                    net_amount: newOrder.netAmount,\n                    note: newOrder.note,\n                    delivery_address: newOrder.deliveryAddress,\n                    delivery_zone: newOrder.deliveryZone,\n                    delivery_fee: newOrder.deliveryFee,\n                    payment_method: newOrder.paymentMethod,\n                    pickup_time: newOrder.pickupTime,\n                    table_number: newOrder.tableNumber,\n                    items: newOrder.items\n                }]);\n\n                if (error) {\n                    console.error(\"Supabase Order Insert Error:\", error);\n                }\n            } catch (err) {\n                console.error(\"Supabase Connection Error (Swallowed):\", err);\n                // Swallow \"Failed to fetch\" errors here so app continues offline\n            }\n        }\n\n        clearCart();\n        return true;\n    } catch (criticalError) {\n        console.error(\"Critical Error in placeOrder:\", criticalError);\n        alert(\"An unexpected error occurred, but we are attempting to process your request locally.\");\n        return true; // Return true to close UI even if critical error logic happens\n    }\n  };\n\n  const updateOrderStatus = async (orderId: string, status: Order['status']) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n             await supabase.from('orders').update({ status }).eq('id', orderId);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Status update error\", e); }\n      }\n      setOrders(prev => prev.map(o => o.id === orderId ? { ...o, status } : o));\n  };\n  \n  // NEW: Complete Order with Payment Update\n  const completeOrder = async (orderId: string, paymentDetails: { paymentMethod: PaymentMethod, note?: string }) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n             await supabase.from('orders').update({ \n                 status: 'completed',\n                 payment_method: paymentDetails.paymentMethod,\n                 note: paymentDetails.note // Append or overwrite note\n             }).eq('id', orderId);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Complete order error\", e); }\n      }\n      // Update Local\n      setOrders(prev => prev.map(o => o.id === orderId ? { \n          ...o, \n          status: 'completed',\n          paymentMethod: paymentDetails.paymentMethod,\n          note: paymentDetails.note ? (o.note ? o.note + ' ' + paymentDetails.note : paymentDetails.note) : o.note\n      } : o));\n  };\n  \n  const deleteOrder = async (orderId: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n             await supabase.from('orders').delete().eq('id', orderId);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Delete order error\", e); } catch(e) { console.error(\"Expense add error\", e); }\n      }\n      // Always local update\n      setExpenses(prev => [...prev, expense]);\n  };\n  const deleteExpense = async (id: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try { await supabase.from('expenses').delete().eq('id', id); }\n      }\n      setStoreSettings({ ...storeSettings, isOpen, closedMessage: message });\n  };\n  \n  const updateStoreSettings = async (settings: Partial<StoreSettings>) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            // Convert camelCase to snake_case for DB\n            const dbPayload: any = { id: 'global' }; // Ensure ID is present for upsert\n            \n            if (settings.holidayStart !== undefined) dbPayload.holiday_start = settings.holidayStart;\n            if (settings.holidayEnd !== undefined) dbPayload.holiday_end = settings.holidayEnd;\n            if (settings.promoBannerUrl !== undefined) dbPayload.promo_banner_url = settings.promoBannerUrl;\n            if (settings.promoContentType !== undefined) dbPayload.promo_content_type = settings.promoContentType;\n            // New fields\n            if (settings.reviewUrl !== undefined) dbPayload.review_url = settings.reviewUrl;\n            if (settings.facebookUrl !== undefined) dbPayload.facebook_url = settings.facebookUrl;\n            if (settings.lineUrl !== undefined) dbPayload.line_url = settings.lineUrl;\n            if (settings.mapUrl !== undefined) dbPayload.map_url = settings.mapUrl;\n            if (settings.contactPhone !== undefined) dbPayload.contact_phone = settings.contactPhone;\n            \n            // Arrays\n            if (settings.reviewLinks !== undefined) dbPayload.review_links = settings.reviewLinks;\n            if (settings.vibeLinks !== undefined) dbPayload.vibe_links = settings.vibeLinks;\n            if (settings.newsItems !== undefined) dbPayload.news_items = settings.newsItems;\n\n            await supabase.from('store_settings').upsert(dbPayload); // Changed to UPSERT for reliability\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Settings sync error\", e); }\n      }\n      setStoreSettings(prev => ({...prev, ...settings}));\n  };\n  \n  const generateTimeSlots = (dateOffset: number = 0) => {\n      const slots: string[] = [];\n      const startHour = OPERATING_HOURS.open; // 11\n      const endHour = OPERATING_HOURS.close; // 20.5 (8:30 PM)\n\n      const now = new Date();\n      // Current hour in decimal (e.g. 14.5 for 2:30 PM)\n      const currentHour = now.getHours() + now.getMinutes() / 60;\n\n      for (let h = startHour; h <= endHour; h += 0.5) {\n          // If ordering for Today (offset 0)\n          if (dateOffset === 0) {\n              // 1. }));\n      } catch (e) {\n          console.error(\"Export failed\", e);\n          return [];\n      }\n  };\n  \n  const customerLogin = async (phone: string, password: string): Promise<boolean> => Please run SQL script.\");\n                  return;\n              }\n          }\n          if (data) setOrders(data.map(d => ({\n              ...d, \n              customerName: d.customer_name, \n              customerPhone: d.customer_phone, \n              totalAmount: d.total_amount,\n              netAmount: d.net_amount || d.total_amount,\n              createdAt: d.created_at,\n              deliveryAddress: d.delivery_address,\n              deliveryZone: d.delivery_zone,\n              deliveryFee: d.delivery_fee,\n              paymentMethod: d.payment_method,\n              pickupTime: d.pickup_time,\n              tableNumber: d.table_number\n          })));\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Orders fetch failed\", err); \n            clearInterval(interval);\n        }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update customer profile on load if logged in\n  useEffect(() => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured && customer) {\n          fetchCustomerProfile();\n      }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Actions\n  const addPizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').insert([{\n                id: pizza.id, name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }]);\n          } catch (e) { console.error(e); (item: CartItem) => setCart(prev => [...prev, item]);\n  const updateCartItemQuantity = (itemId: string, delta: number) => {\n      setCart(prev => prev.map(item => {\n          if (item.id === itemId) {\n              const newQty = Math.max(1, item.quantity + delta);\n              return { ...item, quantity: newQty, totalPrice: (item.totalPrice / item.quantity) * newQty };\n          }\n          return item;\n      }));\n  };\n  const updateCartItem = (updatedItem: CartItem) => {\n      setCart(prev => prev.map(item => item.id === updatedItem.id ? updatedItem : item));\n  };\n  const  \n            if (profile.pdpaAccepted !== undefined) payload.pdpa_accepted = profile.pdpaAccepted;\n            if (profile.savedAddresses !== undefined) payload.saved_addresses =         if (data) {\n                  // User exists! Preserve their valuable data\n                  action = 'updated';\n                  existingPoints = data.loyalty_points || 0;\n                  existingHistory = data.order_history || [];\n                  existingFavorites = data.saved_favorites || [];\n                  existingTier = data.tier;\n              }\n          } catch (e) { console.warn(\"Error checking existing customer\", e); orderHistory: existingHistory,\n          savedFavorites: existingFavorites,\n          tier: existingTier\n      };\n      \n      await setCustomer(finalProfile);\n      return action;\n  };\n  \n  const getAllCustomers = async () => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) return [];\n      try {\n          const { data, error } = await supabase.from('customers').select('name, phone, loyalty_points, Birthday: c.birthday,\n              Address: c.address ? c.address.replace(/[\\n,]/g, ' ') : '', // Escape commas\n              OrdersCount: c.order_history ? c.order_history.length : 0\n          }));\n      } catch (e) {\n          console.error(\"Export failed\", e);\n          return [];\n      }\n  };\n  \n  const customerLogin = async (phone: string, password: string): Promise<boolean> => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          // If DB is offline, check local storage or basic bypass for demo purposes\n          const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_customer');\n          if (saved) {\n              const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);\n              if (parsed.phone === phone) { // Very basic \"offline\" check\n                  setCustState(parsed);\n                  return true;\n              }\n          }\n          alert(\"Database not connected and no local profile found.\");\n          return false;\n      }\n      try {\n          const { data, error } = {\n          console.error(\"Login failed\", e);\n      }\n      return false;\n  };\n\n  const addToFavorites = async (name: string, pizzaId: string, toppings: Topping[]) => {\n      if (!customer) addToCart({\n          id: 'reward-' + Date.now(),\n          pizzaId: pizza.id,\n          name: `🏆 FREE ${pizza.name}`,\n          nameTh: `🏆 ฟรี ${pizza.nameTh || pizza.name}`,\n          basePrice: 0,\n          selectedToppings: [],\n          quantity: 1,\n          totalPrice: 0\n      });\n      // Deduct points\n      const updated = { ...customer, loyaltyPoints: customer.loyaltyPoints - 10 };\n      setCustomer(updated);\n      return true;\n  };\n\n  // Orders\n  const placeOrder = async (type: OrderType, details: any = {}): Promise<boolean> => {\n    // If DB is offline, we proceed with local state to allow the app to function as a demo/offline POS\n    try {\n        const { note, delivery, paymentMethod, pickupTime, tableNumber, source = 'store', status } = details;\n        \n        // Save address if new (only for store orders with a logged in customer)\n        if (source === 'store' && customer && type === 'delivery' && delivery?.address) {\n            const currentSaved = customer.savedAddresses || [];\n            if (!currentSaved.includes(delivery.address)) {\n                const newSavedAddresses = [...currentSaved, delivery.address];\n                // Note: setCustomer handles its own errors silently\n                try {\n                     await setCustomer({ ...customer, savedAddresses: Revenue (Deduct GP)\n        const gpRate = GP_RATES[source as OrderSource] || 0;\n        const netAmount = cartTotal * (1 - gpRate);\n\n        const newOrder: Order = {\n            id: Date.now().toString(),\n            customerName: customer?.name || 'Guest',\n            customerPhone: customer?.phone || 'Guest',\n            type,\n            source: source,\n            // Use Find Order locally\n    const order = orders.find(o => o.id === orderId);\n    if (!order) return;\n\n    // 2. Prepare Updates\n    const updatedOrder = { \n        ...order, \n        status: 'completed' as OrderStatus, \n        paymentMethod: paymentDetails.paymentMethod,\n        note: (order.note ? order.note + '. ' : '') + (paymentDetails.note || '')\n    };\n    \n    // 3. Update Local State Immediately\n    setOrders(prev => prev.map(o => o.id === orderId ? updatedOrder : o));\n\n    // 4. to LocalStorage\n  useEffect(() => {\n      localStorage.setItem('damac_menu', JSON.stringify(menu));\n  }, [menu]);\n\n  const [toppings, setToppings] = useState<Topping[]>(INITIAL_TOPPINGS);\n  const [orders, setOrders] = useState<Order[]>([]);\n  const [expenses, setExpenses] = useState<Expense[]>([]);\n  const [cart, setCart] = useState<CartItem[]>([]);\n  const [customer, setCustState] = useState<CustomerProfile | null>(() => {\n    const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_customer');\n    return saved ? JSON.parse(saved) : null;\n  });\n\n  // --- Store Settings State (From DB + Local Storage Backup) ---\n  const [storeSettings, setStoreSettings] = useState<StoreSettings>(() => {\n      if (typeof useEffect(() => {\n      localStorage.setItem('damac_store_settings', JSON.stringify(storeSettings));\n  }, [storeSettings]);\n\n  const [isHoliday, setIsHoliday] = useState(false);\n  const [isStoreOpen, setIsStoreOpen] = useState(true);\n\n  // Helper to check if today is within holiday range\n  const checkHolidayStatus = (start?: string, end?: string) => {\n      if (!start || !end) return false;\n      const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];\n      return today >= start && today <= end;\n  };\n\n  const checkOperatingHours = () => {\n    const now = new Date();\n    const currentHour = now.getHours() + now.getMinutes() / 60;\n    const isOpenHours = currentHour >= OPERATING_HOURS.open && currentHour < OPERATING_HOURS.close;\n    return isOpenHours;\n  };\n  \n  const canOrderForToday = () => {\n      const now = new Date();\n      const currentHour = now.getHours() + now.getMinutes() / 60;\n      // Can order today if we haven't passed the closing time yet\n      return currentHour < OPERATING_HOURS.close;\n  };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n     // Check if explicit holiday in DB OR manually closed\n     const isScheduledHoliday = checkHolidayStatus(storeSettings.holidayStart, storeSettings.holidayEnd);\n     const effectiveHoliday = isScheduledHoliday || !storeSettings.isOpen;\n     \n     // Store is \"Open\" if no holiday/manual close AND within hours\n     const withinHours = checkOperatingHours();\n     \n     setIsHoliday(isScheduledHoliday);\n     // Note: isStoreOpen tracks \"Currently accepting ASAP orders\". \n     // If closed (morning), you can still preorder for today.\n     setIsStoreOpen(!effectiveHoliday && withinHours);\n  }, [storeSettings]);\n\n  // DB Sync\n  const fetchMenu = async () => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) return;\n      try {\n        const { data, error } = await supabase.from('menu_items').select('*');\n        if (!error && data) {\n           // Merge with local to ensure category/combo logic exists even if DB column missing\n           const mergedMenu = data.map(d => {\n               const local = INITIAL_MENU.find(m => m.id === d.id);\n               return {\n                   ...d, \n                   basePrice: d.base_price, \n                   nameTh: d.name_th, \n                   descriptionTh: d.description_th, \n                   isBestSeller: d.is_best_seller,\n                   comboCount: d.combo_count !== undefined ? d.combo_count : (local?.comboCount || 0),\n                   category: d.category || local?.category || 'pizza'\n               };\n           });\n           setMenu(mergedMenu);\n        }\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Menu fetch failed\", err); }\n  };\n  const fetchToppings = async () => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) return;\n      try {\n          const { data, error } = await supabase.from('toppings').select('*');\n          if (!error && data) {\n              const mergedToppings = data.map(d => {\n                  const local = INITIAL_TOPPINGS.find(t => t.id === d.id);\n                  return {\n                      ...d, \n                      nameTh: d.name_th,\n                      category: d.category || local?.category || 'other',\n                      image: d.image || undefined,\n                      available: d.available !== false // Default true if null/undefined\n                  };\n              });\n              setToppings(mergedToppings);\n          }\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Toppings fetch failed\", err); ascending: false });\n          if (error) {\n              if (error.code === '42P01') {\n                  console.warn(\"Table 'orders' missing. Please run SQL script.\");\n                  return;\n              }\n          }\n          if (data) setOrders(data.map(d => ({\n              ...d, \n              customerName: d.customer_name, \n              customerPhone: d.customer_phone, \n              totalAmount: d.total_amount,\n              netAmount: d.net_amount || d.total_amount,\n              createdAt: d.created_at,\n              deliveryAddress: d.delivery_address,\n              deliveryZone: d.delivery_zone,\n              deliveryFee: d.delivery_fee,\n              paymentMethod: d.payment_method,\n              pickupTime: d.pickup_time,\n              tableNumber: d.table_number\n          })));\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Orders fetch failed\", err); // Reload orders when change happens\n        })\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'menu_items' }, fetchMenu)\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'toppings' }, fetchToppings) // Subscribe to toppings\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'store_settings' }, fetchSettings)\n        .subscribe();\n        \n        // Polling fallback every 5 seconds to ensure status updates even if realtime is flaky\n        const interval = setInterval(() => {\n             fetchOrders();\n        }, 5000);\n        \n        return () => { \n            subscription.unsubscribe(); \n            clearInterval(interval);\n        }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update customer profile on load if logged in\n  useEffect(() => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured && customer) {\n          fetchCustomerProfile();\n      }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Actions\n  const addPizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').insert([{\n                id: pizza.id, name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }]);\n          } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\n      } \n      // Always update local state for immediate feedback\n      setMenu(prev => [...prev, pizza]);\n  };\n  const updatePizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').update({\n                name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }).eq('id', pizza.id);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); newSavedAddresses = [details.delivery.address, ...newSavedAddresses].slice(0, 5); // Keep last 5\n              }\n          }\n\n          const updatedCustomer = { \n              ...customer, \n              loyaltyPoints: newPoints, \n              orderHistory: newHistory,\n              savedAddresses: newSavedAddresses\n          };\n          await setCustomer(updatedCustomer);\n      }\n      \n      // Clear Cart if online/delivery or if specifically requested (Store orders might keep cart for next? ' + paymentDetails.note : paymentDetails.note) : o.note\n      } : o));\n  };\n\n  const deleteOrder = async (orderId: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          await       } else {\n            url.searchParams.set('view', view);\n        }\n        // Preserve table param if it exists\n        if (tableSession) {\n            url.searchParams.set('table', const canOrderForToday = () => {\n      const now = new Date();\n      const currentHour = now.getHours() + now.getMinutes() / 60;\n      // Can order today if we haven't passed the closing time yet\n found.savedAddresses;\n                   action = 'updated';\n               }\n           }\n      }\n\n      const finalProfile: CustomerProfile = {\n          ...newProfile,\n          loyaltyPoints: existingPoints,\n          orderHistory: existingHistory,\n          savedFavorites: existingFavorites,\n          tier: existingTier,\n          savedAddresses: {\n          const { data, error } = await supabase.from('toppings').select('*');\n          if (!error && data) {\n              const mergedToppings = data.map(d => {\n                  const local = INITIAL_TOPPINGS.find(t => t.id === d.id);\n                  return {\n                      ...d, \n                      nameTh: d.name_th,\n                      category: d.category || local?.category || 'other',\n                      image: d.image || undefined,\n                      available: d.available !== false // Default true if null/undefined\n                  };\n              });\n              setToppings(mergedToppings);\n          }\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Toppings fetch failed\", err); }\n  };\n  const fetchOrders = async () => {\n      if    if (error.code === '42P01') {\n                  console.warn(\"Table 'orders' missing. Please run SQL script.\");\n                  return;\n              }\n          }\n          if (data) setOrders(data.map(d => ({\n              ...d, \n              customerName: d.customer_name, \n              customerPhone: d.customer_phone, \n              totalAmount: d.total_amount,\n              netAmount: d.net_amount || d.total_amount,\n              createdAt: d.created_at,\n              deliveryAddress: d.delivery_address,\n              deliveryZone: d.delivery_zone,\n              deliveryFee: d.delivery_fee,\n              paymentMethod: d.payment_method,\n              pickupTime: d.pickup_time,\n              tableNumber: d.table_number\n          })));\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Orders fetch failed\", err); }\n          }\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Profile fetch failed\", err); }\n  }\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n        fetchMenu();\n        fetchToppings();\n        fetchOrders();\n        fetchSettings();\n        \n        const subscription = supabase.channel('realtime_updates')\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'orders' }, (payload) => {\n            fetchOrders(); // Reload orders when change happens\n        })\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'menu_items' }, fetchMenu)\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'toppings' }, fetchToppings) // Subscribe to toppings\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'store_settings' }, fetchSettings)\n        .subscribe();\n        \n        // Polling fallback every 5 seconds to ensure status updates even if realtime is flaky\n        const interval = setInterval(() => {\n             fetchOrders();\n        }, 5000);\n        \n        return () => { \n            subscription.unsubscribe(); \n            clearInterval(interval);\n        }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update customer profile on load if logged in\n  useEffect(() => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured && customer) {\n          fetchCustomerProfile();\n      }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Actions\n  const addPizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').insert([{\n                id: pizza.id, name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }]);\n          } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\n      } \n      // Always update local state for immediate feedback\n      setMenu(prev => [...prev, pizza]);\n  };\n  const updatePizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').update({\n                name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }).eq('id', pizza.id);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      // Always update local\n      setMenu(prev => prev.map(p => p.id === pizza.id ? pizza : p));\n  };\n  const deletePizza = async (id: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try { await supabase.from('menu_items').delete().eq('id', id); } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setMenu(prev => prev.filter(p => p.id !== id));\n  };\n  const updatePizzaPrice = async (id: string, newPrice: number) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) await updatePizza({ ...p, basePrice: newPrice });\n  };\n  const togglePizzaAvailability = async (id: string) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) await updatePizza({ ...p, available: !p.available });\n  };\n  const toggleBestSeller = async (id: string) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) {\n          const newVal = !p.isBestSeller;\n          if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n              try {\n                await supabase.from('menu_items').update({ is_best_seller: newVal }).eq('id', id);\n              } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n          }\n          setMenu(prev => prev.map(item => item.id === id ? {...item, isBestSeller: newVal} : item));\n      }\n  }\n\n  const generateLuckyPizza = () => {\n      const pizzaBase = menu.find(p => p.name.includes(\"Create Your Own\"));\n      if (!pizzaBase) return null;\n      \n      const randomToppings: Topping[] = [];\n      const numToppings = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 2; Cannot upload.\");\n          return;\n      }\n      const confirmUpload = window.confirm(\"This will upload all the latest Menu Items and Toppings from the code to the Database. It will overwrite existing items with the same ID. Continue?\");\n      if (!confirmUpload) return;\n\n      try {\n          // Upload Menu\n          for (const p of INITIAL_MENU) {\n              const { error } = await supabase.from('menu_items').upsert({\n                  id: p.id, name: p.name, name_th: p.nameTh, \n                  base_price: p.basePrice, description: p.description, \n                  description_th: p.descriptionTh, image: p.image, \n                  category: p.category, available: p.available, \n                  is_best_seller: p.isBestSeller, combo_count: p.comboCount\n              });\n              if (error) console.error(\"Menu Seed Error\", error);\n          }\n          // Upload Toppings\n          for (const t of INITIAL_TOPPINGS) {\n              const { error } = await supabase.from('toppings').upsert({\n                  id: t.id, name: t.name, name_th: t.nameTh, price: t.price,\n                  category: t.category, image: t.image, available: t.available\n              });\n              if (error) console.error(\"Topping Seed Error\", error);\n          }\n          alert(\"Menu uploaded to database successfully! Your app is now in sync.\");\n          fetchMenu(); // Refresh\n          fetchToppings(); // Refresh\n      } catch (err) {\n          console.error(\"Seeding failed\", err);\n          alert(\"Seeding failed. Check console for details.\");\n      }\n  };\n\n  const addTopping = async (topping: Topping) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('toppings').insert([{\n                id: topping.id, name: topping.name, name_th: topping.nameTh, price: topping.price, \n                category: topping.category, image: topping.image, available: topping.available\n            }]);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setToppings(prev => [...prev, topping]);\n  };\n  \n  const updateTopping = async (topping: Topping) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('toppings').update({\n                name: topping.name, name_th: topping.nameTh, price: topping.price, \n                category: topping.category, image: topping.image, available: topping.available\n            }).eq('id', topping.id);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setToppings(prev => prev.map(t => t.id === topping.id ? topping : t));\n  };\n\n  const deleteTopping = async (id: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try { await supabase.from('toppings').delete().eq('id', id); } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setToppings(prev => prev.filter(t => t.id !== id));\n  };\n  \n  // Cart\n  const addToCart = (item: CartItem) => setCart(prev => [...prev, item]);\n  const updateCartItemQuantity = (itemId: string, delta: number) => {\n      setCart(prev => prev.map(item => {\n          if (item.id === itemId) {\n              const newQty = Math.max(1, item.quantity + delta);\n              return { ...item, quantity: newQty, totalPrice: (item.totalPrice / item.quantity) * newQty };\n          }\n          return item;\n      }));\n  };\n  const updateCartItem = (updatedItem: CartItem) => {\n      setCart(prev => prev.map(item => item.id === updatedItem.id ? updatedItem : item));\n  };\n  const removeFromCart = (itemId: string) => setCart(prev => prev.filter(item => item.id !== itemId));\n  const clearCart = () => setCart([]);\n  const cartTotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.totalPrice, 0);\n\n  // Customer\n  const setCustomer = async (profile: CustomerProfile) => {\n      setCustState(profile);\n      try {\n        localStorage.setItem('damac_customer', JSON.stringify(profile));\n      } catch(e) { console.error(\"Customer Storage Full\", e); }\n      \n      // Update Offline Backup\n      try {\n        const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_mock_customers');\n        let list = saved ? JSON.parse(saved) : [];\n        list = list.filter((c: any) => c.phone !== profile.phone);\n        list.push(profile);\n        localStorage.setItem('damac_mock_customers', JSON.stringify(list));\n      } catch(e) { console.error(\"Mock Customer Storage Full\", e); }\n\n      // Sync to DB if connected\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            const payload: any = {\n                phone: profile.phone, \n                name: profile.name, \n                address: profile.address, \n                birthday: profile.birthday, \n                password: profile.password,\n                loyalty_points: profile.loyaltyPoints, \n                tier: profile.tier,\n                saved_favorites: profile.savedFavorites, \n                order_history: profile.orderHistory\n            };\n            \n            if (profile.pdpaAccepted !== undefined) payload.pdpa_accepted = profile.pdpaAccepted;\n            if => {\n      let existingPoints = 0;\n      let existingHistory: string[] = [];\n      let existingFavorites: SavedFavorite[] = [];\n      let existingTier: 'Bronze' | 'Silver' | 'Gold' | undefined = undefined;\n      let existingSavedAddresses: string[] = [];\n      let action: 'created' | 'updated' = 'created';\n\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          // Check if user exists\n          try {\n              const { data } = await supabase.from('customers').select('*').eq('phone', newProfile.phone).single();\n              if (data) {\n                  existingPoints =               existingSavedAddresses = data.saved_addresses || [];\n                  action = 'updated';\n              }\n          } catch(e) {}\n      } else {\n           // Local Storage fallback for mock\n           const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_mock_customers');\n           if (saved) {\n               const list = JSON.parse(saved);\n               const found =                  existingFavorites = found.savedFavorites;\n                   existingTier = found.tier;\n                   existingSavedAddresses = found.savedAddresses;\n                   action = 'updated';\n               }\n           }\n      }\n\n      const finalProfile: CustomerProfile = {\n          ...newProfile,\n          loyaltyPoints: existingPoints,\n          orderHistory: // First try DB if connected\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          const { data } = await supabase.from('customers').select('*').eq('phone', phone).single();\n          if (data && } catch(e) { console.error(\"Login Storage Error\", e); }\n              return true;\n          }\n      } \n      \n      // Fallback to local mock data (for testing or offline)\n      const saved =   let localCustomers = [];\n\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          const { data } = await supabase.from('customers').select('*');\n          if (data) dbCustomers = data;\n      }\n      \n removing duplicates based on phone\n      const combined = [...dbCustomers];\n      for (const local of localCustomers) {\n          if (!combined.find(c => c.phone === local.phone)) {\n              combined.push(local);\n          }\n      }\n      \n      return combined;\n  }\n\n  const addToFavorites = async (name: string, pizzaId: string, toppings: Topping[]) => {\n      if (!customer) const updatedCustomer = { ...customer, loyaltyPoints: customer.loyaltyPoints - 10 };\n      setCustomer(updatedCustomer);\n      return true;\n  };\n\n  // Orders\n  const placeOrder = async (\n    type: OrderType, \n    details?: {\n      note?: string;\n      delivery?: { address: string; zoneName: string; fee: number };\n      paymentMethod?: PaymentMethod;\n      pickupTime?: string;\n      tableNumber?: string;\n      source?: OrderSource;\n      status?: OrderStatus;\n    }\n  ) => {\n      // Calculate Total\n      const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.totalPrice, 0);\n      const deliveryFee = details?.delivery?.fee || 0;\n      const totalAmount = subtotal + deliveryFee;\n      \n      // Calculate Net (GP Deduction)\n      const source = details?.source || 'store';\n      const gpRate = GP_RATES[source] || 0;\n      const netAmount = totalAmount * (1 - gpRate);\n\n      const newOrder: Order = {\n          id: Date.now().toString(),\n          customerName: customer ? customer.name : (details?.tableNumber ? `Table ${details.tableNumber}` : 'Guest'),\n          customerPhone: customer ? customer.phone : '',\n          type,\n          source: source,\n          status: details?.status || 'pending',\n          items: [...cart],\n          totalAmount,\n          netAmount,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n          note: details?.note,\n          deliveryAddress: details?.delivery?.address,\n          deliveryZone: details?.delivery?.zoneName,\n          deliveryFee: details?.delivery?.fee,\n          paymentMethod: details?.paymentMethod,\n          pickupTime: details?.pickupTime,\n          tableNumber: details?.tableNumber\n      };\n\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n             const payload: any = {\n                 id: newOrder.id,\n                 customer_name: newOrder.customerName,\n                 customer_phone: newOrder.customerPhone,\n                 type:              delivery_zone: newOrder.deliveryZone,\n                 delivery_fee: newOrder.deliveryFee,\n                 payment_method: newOrder.paymentMethod,\n                 pickup_time: newOrder.pickupTime,\n                 table_number: newOrder.tableNumber\n             };\n             await supabase.from('orders').insert([payload]);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Order localStorage.setItem('damac_last_order', newOrder.id);\n      } catch(e) {}\n      \n      // Update Customer (Loyalty + History + Saved Address)\n      if (customer) {\n          // Loyalty: 1 point per pizza item\n          const pizzaCount = cart.filter(i => {\n               const itemDef = menu.find(m => m.id === i.pizzaId);\n               return itemDef?.category === 'pizza' || itemDef?.category === 'promotion';\n          }).reduce((sum, i) => sum + i.quantity, 0);\n\n          let newPoints = customer.loyaltyPoints + pizzaCount;\n          const newHistory = [newOrder.id, ...customer.orderHistory];\n          \n          let newSavedAddresses = customer.savedAddresses || [];\n          if (type === 'delivery' && details?.delivery?.address) {\n              if (!newSavedAddresses.includes(details.delivery.address)) {\n                  newSavedAddresses = [details.delivery.address, ...newSavedAddresses].slice(0, 5); // Keep last 5\n              }\n          }\n\n          const updatedCustomer = { \n              ...customer, \n              loyaltyPoints: newPoints, \n              orderHistory: newHistory,\n              savedAddresses: ' + paymentDetails.note : paymentDetails.note) : o.note\n      } : o));\n  };\n\n  const deleteOrder = async (orderId: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          await orders.find(o => o.id === orderId);\n      if (order) {\n          order.items.forEach(item => {\n               addToCart({ ...item, id: Date.now() + Math.random().toString() });\n          });\n      }\n  };\n\n  // Expenses\n  const addExpense = async (expense: Expense) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          // Assuming 'expenses' table exists\n          await 'pizza',\n                   available: d.available\n               };\n           });\n           setMenu(mergedMenu);\n        }\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Menu fetch failed\", err); }\n  };\n\n  const fetchToppings = async () => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) return;\n      try {\n          const { data, error } = await supabase.from('toppings').select('*');\n          if (!error && data) {\n              // PRESERVE LOCAL IMAGES for Toppings\n              let localToppings: Topping[] = [];\n              try {\n                  const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_toppings');\n                  if (saved) localToppings = JSON.parse(saved);\n              } catch(e) {}\n\n              const mergedToppings = data.map(d => {\n                  const local = INITIAL_TOPPINGS.find(t => t.id === d.id);\n                  const savedLocal = localToppings.find(t => t.id === d.id);\n                  return {\n                      ...d, setToppings(mergedToppings);\n          }\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Toppings fetch failed\", err); }\n  };\n\n  const fetchOrders = async () => {\n      if (!isSupabaseConfigured) '42P01') {\n                  console.warn(\"Table 'orders' missing. Please run SQL script.\");\n                  return;\n              }\n          }\n          if (data) setOrders(data.map(d => ({\n              ...d, \n              customerName: d.customer_name, \n              customerPhone: d.customer_phone, \n              totalAmount: d.total_amount,\n              netAmount: d.net_amount || d.total_amount,\n              createdAt: d.created_at,\n              deliveryAddress: d.delivery_address,\n              deliveryZone: d.delivery_zone,\n              deliveryFee: d.delivery_fee,\n              paymentMethod: d.payment_method,\n              pickupTime: d.pickup_time,\n              tableNumber: d.table_number\n          })));\n      } catch (err) { console.error(\"Orders fetch failed\", err); // Reload orders when change happens\n        })\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'menu_items' }, fetchMenu)\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'toppings' }, fetchToppings) // Subscribe to toppings\n        .on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'store_settings' }, fetchSettings)\n        .subscribe();\n        \n        // Polling fallback every 5 seconds to ensure status updates even if realtime is flaky\n        const interval = setInterval(() => {\n             fetchOrders();\n        }, 5000);\n        \n        return () => { \n            subscription.unsubscribe(); \n            clearInterval(interval);\n        }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update customer profile on load if logged in\n  useEffect(() => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured && customer) {\n          fetchCustomerProfile();\n      }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Actions\n  const addPizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').insert([{\n                id: pizza.id, name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }]);\n          } catch (e) { console.error(e); }\n      } \n      // Always update local state for immediate feedback\n      setMenu(prev => [...prev, pizza]);\n  };\n  const updatePizza = async (pizza: Pizza) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('menu_items').update({\n                name: pizza.name, name_th: pizza.nameTh, \n                description: pizza.description, description_th: pizza.descriptionTh,\n                base_price: pizza.basePrice, image: pizza.image, available: pizza.available, category: pizza.category,\n                combo_count: pizza.comboCount\n            }).eq('id', pizza.id);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      // Always update local\n      setMenu(prev => prev.map(p => p.id === pizza.id ? pizza : p));\n  };\n  const deletePizza = async (id: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try { await supabase.from('menu_items').delete().eq('id', id); } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setMenu(prev => prev.filter(p => p.id !== id));\n  };\n  const updatePizzaPrice = async (id: string, newPrice: number) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) await updatePizza({ ...p, basePrice: newPrice });\n  };\n  const togglePizzaAvailability = async (id: string) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) await updatePizza({ ...p, available: !p.available });\n  };\n  const toggleBestSeller = async (id: string) => {\n      const p = menu.find(i => i.id === id);\n      if (p) {\n          const newVal = !p.isBestSeller;\n          if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n              try {\n                await supabase.from('menu_items').update({ is_best_seller: newVal }).eq('id', id);\n              } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n          }\n          setMenu(prev => prev.map(item => item.id === id ? {...item, isBestSeller: newVal} : item));\n      }\n  }\n\n  const generateLuckyPizza = () => {\n      const pizzaBase = menu.find(p => p.name.includes(\"Create Your Own\"));\n      if (!pizzaBase) return null;\n      \n      const randomToppings: Topping[] = [];\n      const numToppings = Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 2; Cannot upload.\");\n          return;\n      }\n      const confirmUpload = window.confirm(\"This will upload all the latest Menu Items and Toppings from the code to the Database. It will overwrite existing items with the same ID. Continue?\");\n      if (!confirmUpload) return;\n\n      try {\n          // Upload Menu\n          for (const p of INITIAL_MENU) {\n              const { error } = await supabase.from('menu_items').upsert({\n                  id: p.id, name: p.name, name_th: p.nameTh, \n                  base_price: p.basePrice, description: p.description, \n                  description_th: p.descriptionTh, image: p.image, \n                  category: p.category, available: p.available, \n                  is_best_seller: p.isBestSeller, combo_count: p.comboCount\n              });\n              if (error) console.error(\"Menu Seed Error\", error);\n          }\n          // Upload Toppings\n          for (const t of INITIAL_TOPPINGS) {\n              const { error } = await supabase.from('toppings').upsert({\n                  id: t.id, name: t.name, name_th: t.nameTh, price: t.price,\n                  category: t.category, image: t.image, available: t.available\n              });\n              if (error) console.error(\"Topping Seed Error\", error);\n          }\n          alert(\"Menu uploaded to database successfully! Your app is now in sync.\");\n          fetchMenu(); // Refresh\n          fetchToppings(); // Refresh\n      } catch (err) {\n          console.error(\"Seeding failed\", err);\n          alert(\"Seeding failed. Check console for details.\");\n      }\n  };\n\n  const addTopping = async (topping: Topping) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('toppings').insert([{\n                id: topping.id, name: topping.name, name_th: topping.nameTh, price: topping.price, \n                category: topping.category, image: topping.image, available: topping.available\n            }]);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setToppings(prev => [...prev, topping]);\n  };\n  \n  const updateTopping = async (topping: Topping) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            await supabase.from('toppings').update({\n                name: topping.name, name_th: topping.nameTh, price: topping.price, \n                category: topping.category, image: topping.image, available: topping.available\n            }).eq('id', topping.id);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(e); }\n      }\n      setToppings(prev => prev.map(t => t.id === topping.id ? updatedItem : item));\n  };\n  const removeFromCart = (itemId: string) => setCart(prev => prev.filter(item => item.id !== itemId));\n  const clearCart = () => setCart([]);\n  const cartTotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.totalPrice, 0);\n\n  // Customer\n  const setCustomer = async (profile: CustomerProfile) => {\n      setCustState(profile);\n      try {\n        localStorage.setItem('damac_customer', JSON.stringify(profile));\n      } catch(e) { console.warn(\"Customer Storage Full\", e); }\n      \n      // Update Offline Backup\n      try {\n        const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_mock_customers');\n        let list = saved ?     } catch(e) { console.warn(\"Mock Customer Storage Full\", e); }\n\n      // Sync to DB if connected\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n            const payload: any = {\n                phone: profile.phone, \n                name: profile.name, \n                address: profile.address, \n                birthday: profile.birthday, \n                password: profile.password,\n                loyalty_points: profile.loyaltyPoints, \n                tier: profile.tier,\n                saved_favorites: profile.savedFavorites, \n                order_history: profile.orderHistory\n            };\n            \n            if (profile.pdpaAccepted !== undefined) payload.pdpa_accepted = profile.pdpaAccepted;\n            if => {\n      let existingPoints = 0;\n      let existingHistory: string[] = [];\n      let existingFavorites: SavedFavorite[] = [];\n      let existingTier: 'Bronze' | 'Silver' | 'Gold' | undefined =               existingSavedAddresses = data.saved_addresses || [];\n                  action = 'updated';\n              }\n          } catch(e) {}\n      } else {\n           // Local Storage fallback for mock\n           const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_mock_customers');\n           if (saved) {\n               const list = JSON.parse(saved);\n               const found =                  existingFavorites = found.savedFavorites;\n                   existingTier = found.tier;\n                   existingSavedAddresses = found.savedAddresses;\n                   action = 'updated';\n               }\n           }\n      }\n\n      const finalProfile: CustomerProfile = {\n          ...newProfile,\n          loyaltyPoints: existingPoints,\n          orderHistory: // First try DB if connected\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          const { data } = await supabase.from('customers').select('*').eq('phone', phone).single();\n          if (data && } catch(e) { console.warn(\"Login Storage Error\", e); }\n              return true;\n          }\n      } \n      \n      // Fallback to local mock data (for testing or offline)\n      const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_mock_customers');\n      if (saved) {\n           const list = JSON.parse(saved);\n           const found = list.find((c: any) => c.phone === phone && c.password ===  let localCustomers = [];\n\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          const { data } = await supabase.from('customers').select('*');\n          if (data) dbCustomers = data;\n      }\n      \n      // Merge with offline data\n      const saved = localStorage.getItem('damac_mock_customers');\n      if (saved) {\n          localCustomers = JSON.parse(saved);\n      }\n\n      // Combine arrays, combined.push(local);\n          }\n      }\n      \n      return combined;\n  }\n\n  const addToFavorites = async (name: string, pizzaId: string, toppings: Topping[]) => {\n      if (!customer) ...customer, savedFavorites: updatedFavs };\n      await setCustomer(updatedCustomer);\n  };\n\n  const claimReward = () => {\n      if (!customer || customer.loyaltyPoints < 10) return false;\n      const updatedCustomer = { ...customer, loyaltyPoints: customer.loyaltyPoints - 10 };\n      setCustomer(updatedCustomer);\n      return true;\n  };\n\n  // Orders\n  const placeOrder = async (\n    type: OrderType, \n    details?: {\n      note?: string;\n      delivery?: { address: string; zoneName: string; fee: number };\n      paymentMethod?: PaymentMethod;\n      pickupTime?: string;\n      tableNumber?: string;\n      source?: OrderSource;\n      status?: OrderStatus;\n    }\n  ) => {\n      // Calculate Total\n      const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.totalPrice, 0);\n      const deliveryFee = details?.delivery?.fee || 0;\n      const totalAmount = subtotal + deliveryFee;\n      \n      // Calculate Net (GP Deduction)\n      const source = details?.source || 'store';\n      const gpRate = GP_RATES[source] || 0;\n      const netAmount = totalAmount * (1 - gpRate);\n\n      const newOrder: Order = {\n          id: Date.now().toString(),\n          customerName: customer ? customer.name : (details?.tableNumber ? `Table ${details.tableNumber}` : 'Guest'),\n          customerPhone: customer ? customer.phone : '',\n          type,\n          source: source,\n          status: details?.status || 'pending',\n          items: [...cart],\n          totalAmount,\n          netAmount,\n          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n          note: details?.note,\n          deliveryAddress: details?.delivery?.address,\n          deliveryZone: details?.delivery?.zoneName,\n          deliveryFee: details?.delivery?.fee,\n          paymentMethod: details?.paymentMethod,\n          pickupTime: details?.pickupTime,\n          tableNumber: details?.tableNumber\n      };\n\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          try {\n             const payload: any = {\n                 id: newOrder.id,\n                 customer_name: newOrder.customerName,\n                 customer_phone: newOrder.customerPhone,\n                 type: newOrder.type,\n                 source: newOrder.source,\n                 status: newOrder.status,\n                 items: newOrder.items,\n                 total_amount: newOrder.totalAmount,\n              delivery_zone: newOrder.deliveryZone,\n                 delivery_fee: newOrder.deliveryFee,\n                 payment_method: newOrder.paymentMethod,\n                 pickup_time: newOrder.pickupTime,\n                 table_number: newOrder.tableNumber\n             };\n             await supabase.from('orders').insert([payload]);\n          } catch(e) { console.error(\"Order placement failed\", e); return false; }\n      }\n\n      setOrders(prev => [newOrder, ...prev]);\n      \n      // Save ID for Guest Tracking\n      try {\n        localStorage.setItem('damac_last_order', newOrder.id);\n      } catch(e) {}\n      \n      // Update Customer (Loyalty + History + Saved Address)\n      if (customer) {\n          // Loyalty: 1 point per pizza item\n          const pizzaCount = cart.filter(i => {\n               const itemDef = menu.find(m => m.id === i.pizzaId);\n               return itemDef?.category === 'pizza' || itemDef?.category === 'promotion';\n          }).reduce((sum, i) => sum + i.quantity, 0);\n\n          let newPoints = customer.loyaltyPoints + pizzaCount;\n          const newHistory = [newOrder.id, ...customer.orderHistory];\n          \n          let newSavedAddresses = customer.savedAddresses || [];\n          if (type === 'delivery' && details?.delivery?.address) {\n              if (!newSavedAddresses.includes(details.delivery.address)) {\n                  newSavedAddresses = [details.delivery.address, ...newSavedAddresses].slice(0, 5); // Keep last 5\n              }\n Overwrite for now or handle logic\n          }).eq('id', orderId);\n      }\n      setOrders(prev => prev.map(o => o.id === orderId ? { \n          ...o, \n          status: 'completed', \n          paymentMethod: paymentDetails.paymentMethod,\n          note: paymentDetails.note ? ' + paymentDetails.note : paymentDetails.note) : o.note\n      } : o));\n  };\n\n  const deleteOrder = async (orderId: string) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          await orders.find(o => o.id === orderId);\n      if (order) {\n          order.items.forEach(item => {\n               addToCart({ ...item, id: Date.now() + Math.random().toString() });\n          });\n      }\n  };\n\n  // Expenses\n  const addExpense = async (expense: Expense) => {\n      if (isSupabaseConfigured) {\n          // Assuming 'expenses' table exists\n          await
